% 2) unicode of the emoji inlorm like: 'U+1F603' or 'U+0031U+FE0FU+20E3' depending on the emoji

% in case image exist use this otherwise use the ':<text>:' form

  \IfFileExists{./#3.png}{\raisebox{-0.1em}{\includegraphics[height=0.9em]{./#3.png}}}{#1}%
}
